// ーーーーーーーーーーーーーーーーーー[end]
[-][-][-][-][-][-][-][-][-][-][-][-][-]
[end]


#ENDMSG()

// these next two labels are printed to indicate whether
// the item is weapon or armor

#ENDMSG()

[end]
